- **Cross-axis vocabulary coherence between strategy tag and extraction strategy is partial — and that's correct** (resolved 2026-05-18 Sprint T5 / CR-6). The two vocabularies describe **different lifecycle stages**: `roaster.strategyTag` is a roaster-default signal (input to Coffee Brief Step 1c, 11 canonicals including directional X→Y shifts + meta-categories SYSTEM / VARIES / SELF-ROASTED); `brews.extraction_strategy` is a brew-resolved outcome (output of the iteration loop, 6 canonicals — no directional, no meta). The 3 brew-side "missing" tags (Suppression / Extraction Push / Hybrid) are correctly absent from roaster-tag space because no roaster bakes them into a house style — they're brew-time decisions driven by the coffee. The 4 roaster-side "extra" tags (SYSTEM / VARIES / BALANCED → X / SELF-ROASTED) are correctly absent from brew-strategy space because every brew resolves to a single strategy. Case-style divergence (UPPERCASE-DASH vs Title Case) encodes which side of the schema the value lives on and is preserved. Recommendation 2 (a cross-mapping table in BREWING.md / wbc-reference.md surfacing typical roaster-tag → brew-strategy patterns) is a future doc-edit ride-along. Full audit at [docs/audits/2026-05-18/CR-6-strategy-tag-extraction-strategy-coherence.md](docs/audits/2026-05-18/CR-6-strategy-tag-extraction-strategy-coherence.md).
- ~~**The SWORKS valve flow taxonomy lives in BREWING.md, not as a `docs/taxonomies/*.md` file**~~ **Resolved 2026-05-18 Sprint T5 / CR-7.** Promoted to a self-only canonical sub-taxonomy alongside EG-1 grinder: [docs/taxonomies/sworks.md](docs/taxonomies/sworks.md) (authoritative authored content) + [lib/sworks-registry.ts](lib/sworks-registry.ts) (validation mirror). Single canonical entry (SWORKS Bottomless Dripper) with per-dial enumerated content (Dial 0 Closed / 1-4 Dead Zone / 5 Restricted / 6 Half-Open / 7 Open / past-7 Maximum Flow), per-dial flow rate calibration, adjustment logic (valve-first), and 5 canonical recipe patterns. Registered as `docs://taxonomies/sworks.md` in MCP catalog (TAXONOMY_AXES list). No `brews` schema column added — registry is a vocabulary anchor; brew-side persistence stays in `brews.pour_structure` free-text. Future structured-pour-structure sprint may promote per-pour valve-dial to a column with validation against `validDials`. Full scoping decision at [docs/audits/2026-05-18/CR-7-sworks-valve-flow-scoping.md](docs/audits/2026-05-18/CR-7-sworks-valve-flow-scoping.md).

- **Roaster could benefit from skeleton-flag adoption** — the `skeleton: true` flag is producer-only today; roaster has a similar "promote-with-thin-content" pattern (Latent roaster entry is effectively a skeleton, several Tier-1h entries had minimal initial content). - **The humanizer pass's preservation list is hardcoded but spot-check-validated** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-16; closed Sprint T4 2026-05-18). Spot-check across 5 cached capsules (Volcán Barú N=24, Ethiopian landrace N=3, Moonwake N=17, Washed-base N=40, Anaerobic-modifier N=16) showed >95% canonical-term survival, including terms outside the hardcoded `USER_OVERRIDE` list ("anoxic", "hermetic tank", "white tea / black tea / orange pekoe") — the humanizer respects domain vocabulary categorically, not just from the explicit allowlist. **Resolved by light-touch expansion**: added one categorical-preservation bullet to `USER_OVERRIDE` covering signature methods (15 canonicals post Sprint T1), fermentation qualifiers ("Anoxic" post Sprint T3 CR-5), and modifier-axis names; kept the existing enumeration as illustrative examples. Build-time CONTEXT.md extraction (Option A) and humanizer tool-use access (Option B) explicitly rejected as over-engineering given the >95% baseline.
- **Synthesis output confidence + length now modulates with corpus size** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-16; closed Sprint T4 2026-05-18 via SYN-2 4-tier classifier). Binary `earlyData` flag retired; replaced with `classifyTier(rowCount)` returning a `TierConfig` carrying paragraph count + takeaway count + `max_tokens` + confidence-language hint per tier. See **Corpus tier** entry for the locked thresholds + per-tier shape. **Mobile short-form variant (SYN-3) stays open** — deferred per master plan; orthogonal to tier modulation (the short-form needs a 2nd LLM-call shape regardless of how long-form sizing works).
- **Synthesis output is too verbose on mobile** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-16; still open post-Sprint-T4). The 4-6 paragraph + 4-6 takeaway shape reads well on desktop but is "really, really long" on mobile. Chris wants a **short-form mobile variant** — "a synthesis of the synthesis" — rendered alongside the long form. Open UX follow-up: scope a 2nd capsule generation (short-form) cached alongside the long form, OR a client-side collapse / truncate-with-expand pattern that doesn't lose the takeaway bullets. The short-form would be a 3rd LLM call shape (digest the long form to ~1-2 paragraphs + 2-3 takeaways) — adds latency + cost; weigh against the truncate-with-expand alternative. Note that Sprint T4's tier-aware sizing helps narrow-corpus capsules naturally (Early-data tier caps at 2-3 paragraphs + 700 tokens) but does NOT solve the mature-tier long-form mobile UX problem.
- **Re-synthesize-don't-append discipline is now a top-of-rules directive** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-16; closed Sprint T4 2026-05-18 via SYN-4). `SHARED_RULES` in [buildPrompt.ts](lib/synthesis/buildPrompt.ts) was restructured: the prior soft "do not summarize each coffee one by one" line is replaced by a directive ("This is a re-synthesis, not a summary. ... The output must NOT have the shape of a list of coffees with one observation per coffee.") + a concrete anti-pattern example ("Anti-pattern: 'In Coffee A I noticed X. In Coffee B I noticed Y...' is appending, not synthesizing."). The two new lines are now positions 1 + 2 in the rules block. Pairs with the **Corpus tier** entry: the mature-tier corpus (16+ coffees) is exactly where appended-list degradation is most likely, so the directive bites hardest where it matters most.
- **No canonical noun for the complete roast recipe specification** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit, round 7). The bundle of inlet curve + fan curve + drop temp + hopper pre-load + end condition + charge temp doesn't have a unified noun in Chris's prose — drifts between "profile" (Roest machine's term), "recipe" (mirrors the `roast_recipes` schema entity), and "spec" (context-dependent). Each component has its own canonical noun (inlet curve, fan curve, etc.) but the *aggregate* is ambiguous. Open question: pick "recipe" as the canonical (aligns with schema), pick "profile" (aligns with Roest machine vocabulary), or leave the context-driven drift in place because the components are distinct enough that the aggregate noun is rarely load-bearing. Mild ambiguity; not urgent.
- **Peer roaster framework lacks structured storage** (resolved 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit, round 6). Peer-roaster cup judgments + design frameworks contribute to V1 design as high-weight directional input (acidity-vs-sweetness axis framework is a primary V2 design lever) but live entirely in Chris's head and in scattered intake notes — peer's resolved roasts aren't in the Roest log and don't get batch numbers like #133 / #139. Open follow-up: scope structured storage for peer-roaster framework (separate `peer_observations` table? structured `notes` field on `green_beans`?) if peer input continues to compound in operational weight. Also: there's no canonical phrase for "this peer observation conflicts with my own anchor-derived data and the conflict is operationally important" — currently resolved by operator judgment with no documented precedence rule. Pairs with the **Signal precedence** entry's storage open question.
- **Roasting carry-forward learnings need an explicit scope-tag dimension** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit, round 6). Brewing's `process_dominant` flag exists at the per-brew level to prevent heavy-process brews from skewing per-cultivar / per-terroir / per-roaster aggregation pages. Roasting's cross-coffee insight layer is already process-segmented by design, so the per-aggregation-page concern doesn't apply — BUT the same concern exists at the **carry-forward learning** layer: not every learning generalizes across process boundaries. Today scope is prose-encoded ("for Sudan Rume Natural" qualifier) with inconsistent tightness — some carry-forwards specify cultivar+process, some specify family-only, some are unscoped. The Sudan Rume Washed → Sudan Rume Natural transition already hit this in practice: washed-anchor carry-forwards from #133 informed Sudan Rume Natural V1 design, and the FC-temp-architectural-constraint hypothesis emerged exactly because some of those carry-forwards didn't transfer. Four resolution options under consideration: (1) per-carry-forward scope tag (structured field on the learning — Chris's instinct), (2) per-lot scoping flag analogous to brewing's process_dominant, (3) extend round-5 precedence framework to handle "this learning doesn't transfer across process families," (4) leave as prose-encoded; accept drift risk at current corpus size. Not urgent at ~5-10 closed lots; revisit when carry-forward corpus crosses a volume threshold similar to where brewing's process_dominant first earned its keep.
- **Brewing signal arbitration is pure precedence; roasting signal arbitration is precedence + weighting (parameter-type-conditional)** (resolved 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit, round 5). Brewing's Coffee Brief Step 1c arbitrates among signals (variety / process / roaster) using precedence — one signal wins the categorical strategy choice. Roasting design produces both categorical decisions (anchor / end condition / drop ceiling regime) and continuous adjustments (peak inlet / fan curve / spread width); the categorical decisions use **Signal precedence**, the continuous adjustments use **Multi-factor weighting**. The cross-project asymmetry is structural: brewing's output is categorical-only (the strategy enum), so precedence-only suffices; roasting's output is mixed, so both frameworks coexist. Brewing-side "signal-override" vocabulary and roasting-side "signal precedence" vocabulary should NOT be conflated — different mechanics, parallel but distinct.
- **ROASTING.md Green-Spec → Starting-Hypothesis table is additive-only; precedence layer is implicit** (Chris-flagged 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit, round 5). The table correctly captures continuous adjustments (density / moisture / altitude rows stack additively) but fails on (i) parameters where multiple signals conflict (low density + natural process — additive math says ~0 net adjustment; precedence says use full natural-anchor energy), and (ii) parameters where one signal categorically rules out a regime another suggests (silent-FC categorically forces bean-temp end condition regardless of what other signals would prefer). Today categorical-precedence is encoded implicitly via anchor selection (pick the right anchor, the protocol comes with it) — works as long as anchors are picked correctly but isn't legible for future-Chris or for claude.ai-the-author. **Doc fix candidate**: add a precedence table to ROASTING.md alongside the additive one — process-family → anchor-selection, FC-audibility-expectation → end-condition, fruit-layer-presence → energy-direction-inversion. Pairs with the **Signal precedence** + **Multi-factor weighting** entries (which capture the framework but don't fix the doc).
- **Schema-vs-writing seam at V-set close-out is deliberately mismatched** (resolved 2026-05-17 via cross-party roasting audit). The experiments table carries per-slot cup-side fields (`observed_outcome_a/b/c/d`, `updated_cup_prediction_a/b/c/d`, `taste_for_a/b/c/d`, `delta_from_cup_a/b/c/d`) suggesting an 18-cell-per-V-set trace structure. Lived practice produces a **V-set-wide cup narrative paragraph** + verdict instead — roast-side metrics decompose to per-slot cells, cup-side observations collapse to one comparative paragraph across slots. Self-reported population rates (CGLE Sudan Rume Natural V2 close-out as the case study): predicted-roast ~20%, actual-roast 100%, roast-delta ~30% (exception-write), predicted-cup-initial ~20%, updated-cup-prediction ~10%, actual-cup 100% as narrative / 0% per-slot, cup-delta 100% as verdict / 0% per-slot. The mismatch is **principled, not drift**: pre-articulated per-slot taste-for biases tasting (single-palate honesty); cup observations are inherently comparative across slots; lever / non-factor promotion is a lot-close artifact, not a V-set close artifact. Three repair options were considered: (a) tighten practice toward 18-cell discipline, (b) collapse schema to V-set-wide cup fields, (c) document the gap and accept it. Locked option: **(c)**. Schema stays as-is; writing produces the V-set close-out narrative; many per-slot cup fields legitimately stay null. **Glossary follow-up**: the trade-off is ADR-worthy (parallel to ADR-0001 / ADR-0002 / proposed ADR-0003); future readers will look at the per-slot schema and wonder why population is so partial. Candidate ADR-0004 (or whichever number is next after the anchor-vocabulary decision lands).
- **Cross-entity knowledge capsules (axis × axis) are out-of-scope by design today, ad-hoc only** (Chris-locked 2026-05-16). The 4 directed-prompt adapters are single-axis (terroir alone / cultivar alone / process alone / roaster alone); no Gesha × Panama or Anaerobic × Heirloom intersection page. Two reasons: (1) combinatorial explosion — 121 macro terroirs × 63 cultivars = 7,623 possible combinations, almost all N=0 or N=1; (2) per-axis capsules already absorb cross-axis signal naturally (a Gesha capsule on a 60%-Panamanian corpus *will* read Panamanian). **Acceptable extensions**: (a) ad-hoc one-off combination capsules Chris might manually request to drill into a specific pairing (workflow note, not a page surface); (b) cross-coffee generalizations that DO span multiple axes live in the **Cross-coffee insight layer** (BREWING.md / ROASTING.md cross-coffee sections), not as code-driven capsules. **Re-test trigger**: a specific combination accumulates strong signal invisible in the per-axis capsule (e.g. "Anaerobic Heirloom is genuinely *its own thing*, distinct from generic Heirloom AND generic Anaerobic").
- **BREWING.md ↔ ROASTING.md cross-coffee section naming asymmetry — naming resolved 2026-05-19 via Sprint 9; structural pass deferred.** BREWING.md's `SECTION 3 — Archive Patterns` was renamed to `Cross-Coffee Insight Layer` to match ROASTING.md (chosen over a third umbrella name — Chris-locked 2026-05-19 as the lighter-touch option). The "be a little bit more structured at exactly what I'm trying to pull out here that is the most helpful for creating new recipes" framing (Chris-articulated 2026-05-16) is **NOT** addressed by Sprint 9 and lives on as a separate queued follow-up: a structural pass on the renamed BREWING.md section (does the body match the ROASTING.md Confirmed Patterns + Working Hypotheses shape? does it surface the right discriminator-for-new-recipes content?). Tracked in PRODUCT.md as a queued sprint, not blocking.
- **Synthesis pipeline subsystem-wide revisit flagged** (Chris-explicit umbrella 2026-05-16): "I probably need to revisit all of this at some point in time. This isn't the perfect final form. I think this was just better than two sentences and good enough." The 3 specific criticisms above (confidence modulation / mobile length / re-synthesize discipline) are concrete instances; the umbrella reserves space for broader rethinks (output format, paragraph count, regeneration trigger semantics, threshold rules) when the corpus grows enough to expose more limitations.
- **Knowledge capsule is brewing-only today; design intent is cross-source** (Chris-explicit 2026-05-16). All 4 synthesis adapters (terroir / cultivar / process / roaster) read `brews` rows only; roasting-side lot-specific learnings + carry-forward learnings on `roast_learnings` rows are NOT in the synthesis corpus. Chris's verbatim intent: "the knowledge capsule should be pulling in both all of the brewing and roasting lessons altogether in one big knowledge capsule, encapsulating all of the various data points." Largest substrate gap surfaced in the synthesis-pipeline grilling. **Open follow-up**: scope a cross-source adapter shape — terroir / cultivar / process adapters should query both `brews` (existing path) AND `roast_learnings` joined through `green_beans.{terroir_id,cultivar_id,signature_method}` for matching lots; roaster adapter is already roughly cross-source via `roaster = 'Latent'` self-roasted brews but doesn't pull `roast_learnings` directly. Schema-wise: the existing data is there; the change is adapter-level + synthesize-route-level (corpus query expansion + new `formatLearningRow` shapes for the roast-side rows).
